 tippaniyan The research results were published in the journal 'international Journal for Equity in Health'

Research found that adults who had no educational qualification were twice as likely (about 150 percent more) to have a heart attack than people with a university degree
 in vayaskon kii aayu 45-64 saal thi
 The risk of heart attack was more than two-thirds (70 percent) among those with intermediate level or non-university education
 isaki vajah yah thi ki acchhee shiksha lambey samay ke swasthya par aapke kaary kii prakruti, aapke rahan-sahan or aapke khaane kii pasand par asar daalati he
 Compared to middle-aged adults who have university degrees, the probability of stroke for the first time was 50 percent among those who did not complete high school and 20 percent among non-university qualification holders
 corda ne kaha ki ek isi tarah kii asamanta gharelu aay or dil kii bimariyon ke bich main bhi pai gai
 The researchers said that this research gives us an opportunity to reveal the special relationship of educational achievement and risk of heart diseases
 isse yah bhi pataa sakegaa ki ise kam karne ke liye kya kiya jaae

 ) For some people, their friends are everything
 ve doston ke bina apni duniya kii kalpana bhi nahin kar pate
 It is important for them to have friends
 par kai baar doston ko milane vaali yah tavajjo unke partner ko pasand nahin aati he
 Many times a partner feels that his personal life is being affected by his partner's friends
 yah naapsandgi dhire-dhire nafrat main badalanaa shuru ho jaati he or iskaa sidhaa asar aapke sambandhon par padataa he
 Before this situation gets worse, it needs to be handled in time
 agar aapkaa partner bhaapane doston ko lekar jarurat se zyada samvedansheel he or aapako lag rahaa heki uskaa yah vyavhaar aapke liye pareshaani kaa kaaran banataa ja rahaa he to aap in tareekon se is samasya kaa samaadhaan dhund sakate hai :1
 Try to change your thinking
 aapako apane partner kii soch ko bhi samajhane kii koshish kerani chahie
 It is possible that after knowing your partner's situation, there will be some change in your thinking
 2
 You should give space to the partner
 is baat ko hameshaa yaad rakhen ki kisi bhi rishte ko banaae rakhane ke liekisi duusare rishte ko chhod dena samajhadaari nahin he or uske saath is mudde par bahes karne se aapkaa hi nuksaan hoga
 3
 is samasya kaa sabase acha samaadhaan yah he ki aap apane partner ke saath baithkar baat karen
 Try to convince him that you too need enough of his time
 par usase bhuulakar bhi yah na kahen ki aapako uskaa hameshaa doston main ghire rahanaa pasand nahin he
 This may affect your relationship
 4
 In such a case you need to act wisely
 koshish kiijie ki aap donon saath main jo bhi vakt bitaayen, vah quality time ho
 It should not be that both of you are quarreling with each other despite being together
 5
 In such times, it is necessary that you work with patience
 aap chahen to apane partner ke doston ko apana bhi dost bana sakate hai
 By doing this, your complaint will also go away because you too can spend time with those friends
 6
 This method is completely based on the science formula
 aap chahen to apane partner kii hi tarah aap bhi apane doston ke saath vyast rahanaa shuru kar sakate hai
 Maybe by seeing the reaction of the action, he will realize this habit which has snatched away your nights sleep
